North_Give_NickName_effect = {
	random_list = {
		990 = {
			modifier = {
				is_male = no
				add = 8
			}
			modifier = {
				is_male = no
				OR = {
					religion = { is_in_family = rf_pagan }
					has_government = tribal_government
				}
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				is_male = yes
				OR = {
					religion = { is_in_family = rf_pagan }
					has_government = tribal_government
				}
				add = 5
			}
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = {
				is_male = yes
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_male = yes
				OR = {
					religion = { is_in_family = rf_pagan }
					has_government = tribal_government
				}
				add = 5
			}
			add_character_flag = got_north_nickname
			norse_pack_nick_name_effect = yes
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = {
				is_male = no
				add = 1
			}
			modifier = {
				is_male = no
				OR = {
					religion = { is_in_family = rf_pagan }
					has_government = tribal_government
				}
				add = 1
			}
			add_character_flag = got_north_nickname
			norse_pack_nick_name_effect = yes
		}
	}

norse_pack_name_ai_male = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_trait = bastard
			}
			exists = father
			father = {
				is_alive = no
			}
		}
		father = {
			save_scope_as = male_ancestor
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				father = {
					exists = dynasty
					dynasty = {
						any_in_list = {
							variable = name_pack_support_dynasty
							this = scope:male_ancestor
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_in_global_list = {
					variable = name_pack_support_global
					this = scope:male_ancestor
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		}
		change_first_name = { template_character = scope:male_ancestor }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_trait = bastard
			}
			exists = father
			father = {
				is_alive = yes
				any_in_list = {
					variable = male_ancestors
					exists = this
				}
			}
		}
		father = {
			random_in_list = {
				variable = male_ancestors
				save_scope_as = male_ancestor
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:male_ancestor = {
					exists = dynasty
					dynasty = {
						any_in_list = {
							variable = name_pack_support_dynasty
							this = scope:male_ancestor
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_in_global_list = {
					variable = name_pack_support_global
					this = scope:male_ancestor
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		}
		change_first_name = { template_character = scope:male_ancestor }
		father = {
			remove_list_variable = { name = male_ancestors target = scope:male_ancestor }
			every_close_family_member = {
				remove_list_variable = { name = male_ancestors target = scope:male_ancestor }
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_trait = bastard
			}
			exists = mother
			mother = {
				is_alive = yes
				any_in_list = {
					variable = male_ancestors
					exists = this
				}
			}
		}
		mother = {
			random_in_list = {
				variable = male_ancestors
				save_scope_as = male_ancestor
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:male_ancestor = {
					exists = dynasty
					dynasty = {
						any_in_list = {
							variable = name_pack_support_dynasty
							this = scope:male_ancestor
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_in_global_list = {
					variable = name_pack_support_global
					this = scope:male_ancestor
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		}
		change_first_name = { template_character = scope:male_ancestor }
		mother = {
			remove_list_variable = { name = male_ancestors target = scope:male_ancestor }
			every_close_family_member = {
				remove_list_variable = { name = male_ancestors target = scope:male_ancestor }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_character_flag = name_pack_support
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				random_list = {
					0 = {

							has_religion = religion:islam_religion

norse_pack_nick_name_effect = {
	save_scope_as = byname_target
	random_list = {
		0 = {
			modifier = {
				age > 55
				add = 5
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Old_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Old2_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
			}
		}
		0 = {
			modifier = {
				add = {
					value = 0.05
					multiply = prowess
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Strong_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Strong2_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Mighty_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Strongface_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Strong3_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = WhaleMight_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = TimberQuaker_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = GreatSlasher_byname target = scope:byname_target }
				}
				1 = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = { name = Strong5_byname target = scope:byname_target }
